### VOLUNTEER DRIVE

![Volunteer Banner](/images/PC_Banner_Volunteer_v2.jpg "Volunteer Drive")

Presidentâ€™s Challenge Volunteer Drive encourages everyone to be more involved in the community and promote volunteerism as a way of life, making Singapore a more caring and compassionate society. The Volunteer Drive promotes the giving of time and skills.


#### PCVD 2022 - Benefitting Agencies' Volunteering Opportunities

<table cellspacing="10px" cellpadding="10px" width="100%">	
<br><b><a href="http://www.odysseydancetheatreltd.com/" target='_blank'>Odyssey Dance Theatre Ltd</a><br></b>
	<b>Volunteers for Programmes, Production & Logistics</b> <br>Odyssey Dance Theatre Ltd is looking for committed, energetic volunteers who can commit regularly in areas of Programmes, Production & Logistics, depending on skills and interest.<br>

<b>Befriender / Cluster Support at St. Andrewâ€™s Adult Home (SAAH) Sengkang</b> <br>SAAH (Sengkang) is looking for volunteers who can:<br>- Befriend residents to encourage socialization and build friendships with the aim of cultivating a supportive and meaningful relationship. <br>- Assist and support care staff and resident support officer in attending to the residents<br>- Assist during community outings <br>- Provide support and supervision to residents to ensure their safety, help them hone relevant skills, and encourage socialisation<br><br>[Induction, online course on ASD and training will be provided. For more information on the roles and responsibilities, kindly contact the email below].
